    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

{
    u_xlat16_0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * vec2(_NormalTilling);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, u_xlat16_0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat1.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat40 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat40 = max(u_xlat40, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat40 = inversesqrt(u_xlat40);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat40) * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz;
    u_xlat40 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz);
    u_xlat40 = max(u_xlat40, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat40 = inversesqrt(u_xlat40);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat40) * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.yyy * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyw = u_xlat16_0.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.zzz * u_xlat1.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyw;
    u_xlat16_39 = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_39 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_39);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_39) * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = texture(_BumpMap1, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat5.yyy;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat5.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat5.zzz * u_xlat1.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_39 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_39 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_39);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_39) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat2.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat3.xy,u_xlat3.z);
    u_xlat2.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat3.xy,u_xlat3.z);
    u_xlat2.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat3.xy,u_xlat3.z);
    u_xlat2.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_39 = dot(u_xlat2, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_43 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_39 * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_43;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb40 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb40 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb40 = u_xlatb40 || u_xlatb2;
    u_xlat16_39 = (u_xlatb40) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_39;
    u_xlat16_6.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_6.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_6.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat40 = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat40 = max(u_xlat40, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat40 = inversesqrt(u_xlat40);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat40) * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(u_xlat40) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_43 = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat16_43 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_43);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_43) * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_43 = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_43 = min(max(u_xlat16_43, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_43 = clamp(u_xlat16_43, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_6.w = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_6.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_6.w = min(max(u_xlat16_6.w, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_6.w = clamp(u_xlat16_6.w, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_7.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_7.x = min(max(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_7.x = clamp(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_20.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);

    u_xlat16_20.x = min(max(u_xlat16_20.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

    u_xlat16_6.x = min(max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0), 1.0);

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_19 = min(max(u_xlat16_19, 0.0), 1.0);

    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * 0.980000019 + 0.0199999996;

    u_xlat16_33 = max(u_xlat16_33, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_33 = min(u_xlat16_33, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_46 = u_xlat16_33 * u_xlat16_33;
    u_xlat16_47 = _RoughnessShine * _RoughnessShine;
    u_xlat16_9.x = (-u_xlat16_19) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xxx;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_19) * u_xlat16_8.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat40 = u_xlat16_4.y * u_xlat16_4.y;
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat16_4.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat40 * 0.125 + u_xlat41;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat3.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat40 = u_xlat40 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat41);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat40 + 0.125;

    u_xlat16_23.xyz = u_xlat16_10.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_23.xyz;
    u_xlat16_48 = dot((-u_xlat2.xyz), u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat16_48 + u_xlat16_48;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_48)) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_7.x = (-u_xlat16_7.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat16_48 * u_xlat16_48;
    u_xlat16_49 = (-u_xlat16_33) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_49 = u_xlat16_33 * u_xlat16_49;
    u_xlat16_49 = u_xlat16_49 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_2 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_11.xyz, u_xlat16_49);
    u_xlat16_49 = u_xlat16_2.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_49 = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_49 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_49 = max(u_xlat16_49, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_49 = log2(u_xlat16_49);
    u_xlat16_49 = u_xlat16_49 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_49 = exp2(u_xlat16_49);
    u_xlat16_49 = u_xlat16_49 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_49);
    u_xlat16_12.xy = vec2(u_xlat16_46) * vec2(u_xlat16_46) + vec2(1.0, -1.0);

    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_46);
    u_xlat16_46 = (-u_xlat16_33) + 1.03999996;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_19 * 0.959999979 + u_xlat16_46;
    u_xlat16_12.xzw = (-u_xlat16_8.xyz) + vec3(u_xlat16_19);
    u_xlat16_12.xzw = vec3(u_xlat16_48) * u_xlat16_12.xzw + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xyz * u_xlat16_12.xzw + u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xy = u_xlat16_6.xw * u_xlat16_6.xw;
    u_xlat16_45 = u_xlat16_47 * u_xlat16_47 + -1.0;

in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_4;
float u_xlat15;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat15 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat15 = max(u_xlat15, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat15 = inversesqrt(u_xlat15);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat15) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * in_TANGENT0.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD8 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

mediump float u_xlat16_45;

void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD0.xy * vec2(_NormalTilling);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, u_xlat16_0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_0.xy = u_xlat16_0.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat1.x = dot(vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = max(u_xlat1.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat1.x);
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz;
    u_xlat40 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat40 = max(u_xlat40, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat40 = inversesqrt(u_xlat40);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat40) * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz;
    u_xlat40 = dot(vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz);
    u_xlat40 = max(u_xlat40, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat40 = inversesqrt(u_xlat40);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat40) * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.yyy * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyw = u_xlat16_0.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.zzz * u_xlat1.xyz + u_xlat16_0.xyw;
    u_xlat16_39 = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_39 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_39);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_39) * u_xlat16_0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = texture(_BumpMap1, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * u_xlat5.yyy;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat5.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat5.zzz * u_xlat1.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_39 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_39 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_39);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_39) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat2.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat3.xy,u_xlat3.z);
    u_xlat2.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat3.xy,u_xlat3.z);
    u_xlat2.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat3.xy,u_xlat3.z);
    u_xlat2.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_39 = dot(u_xlat2, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_43 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_39 * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_43;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb40 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb40 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb2 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb2 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb40 = u_xlatb40 || u_xlatb2;
    u_xlat16_39 = (u_xlatb40) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_39;
    u_xlat16_6.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_6.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_6.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat40 = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat40 = max(u_xlat40, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat40 = inversesqrt(u_xlat40);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat40) * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(u_xlat40) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat16_43 = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat16_43 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_43);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_43) * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_43 = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_43 = min(max(u_xlat16_43, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_43 = clamp(u_xlat16_43, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_6.w = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, u_xlat16_6.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_6.w = min(max(u_xlat16_6.w, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_6.w = clamp(u_xlat16_6.w, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_7.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_7.x = min(max(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_7.x = clamp(u_xlat16_7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_20.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_20.x = min(max(u_xlat16_20.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_20.x = clamp(u_xlat16_20.x, 0.0, 1.0);

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(max(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0), 1.0);

    u_xlat16_6.x = clamp(u_xlat16_6.x, 0.0, 1.0);

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_19 = min(max(u_xlat16_19, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_19 = clamp(u_xlat16_19, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * 0.980000019 + 0.0199999996;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = _BaseColorCenter.xyz + (-_BaseColorCircle.xyz);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * u_xlat16_8.xyz + _BaseColorCircle.xyz;
    u_xlat16_33 = _RoughNessOffset + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_33 = max(u_xlat16_33, 0.0399999991);

    u_xlat16_46 = u_xlat16_33 * u_xlat16_33;

    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xxx;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_19) * u_xlat16_8.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat40 = u_xlat16_4.y * u_xlat16_4.y;
    u_xlat41 = u_xlat16_4.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat40 * 0.125 + u_xlat41;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat3.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat40 = u_xlat40 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat41);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat40 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_10.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_10.xy = u_xlat16_10.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_23.xyz = u_xlat16_10.yyy * _SHBotColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xxx * _SHTopColor.xyz + u_xlat16_23.xyz;
    u_xlat16_48 = dot((-u_xlat2.xyz), u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat16_48 + u_xlat16_48;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_48)) + (-u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_7.x = (-u_xlat16_7.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat16_7.x * u_xlat16_7.x;
    u_xlat16_48 = u_xlat16_48 * u_xlat16_48;
    u_xlat16_49 = (-u_xlat16_33) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_49 = u_xlat16_33 * u_xlat16_49;
    u_xlat16_49 = u_xlat16_49 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_2 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_11.xyz, u_xlat16_49);
    u_xlat16_49 = u_xlat16_2.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_49 = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_49 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_49 = max(u_xlat16_49, 0.0);
